   X509_STORE_set_flags(store, X509_V_FLAG_PARTIAL_CHAIN);\n    89→      bool has_crl = false;\n    90→      for (const X509_INFO* item : list.get()) {\n    91→        if (item->x509) {\n    92→          X509_STORE_add_cert(store, item->x509);\n    93→          if (ca_cert_ == nullptr) {\n    94→            X509_up_ref(item->x509);\n    95→            ca_cert_.reset(item->x509);\n    96→ (!cert_validation_config->subjectAltNameMatchers().empty()) {\n   152→      for (const envoy::extensions::transport_sockets::tls::v3::SubjectAltNameMatcher& matcher :\n   153→ subject_alt_name_matchers_.push_back(std::move(san_matcher));\n   160→      }\n   161→      verify_mode = verify_mode_validation_context;\n   162→    }\n   163→\n   164→    if (!cert_validation_config->verifyCertificateHashList().empty()) {\n   165→      for (auto hash : cert_validation_config->verifyCertificateHashList()) {\n   166→        // Remove colons from the 95 chars long colon-separated \"fingerprint\"\n   167→        // in order to get the hex-encoded string.\n   168→        if (hash.size() == 95) {\n   169→          hash.erase(std::remove(hash.begin(), hash.end(), ':'), hash.end());\n   170→        }\n   171→        const auto& decoded = Hex::decode(hash);\n   172→        if (decoded.size() != SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH) {\n   173→          return verify_mode = verify_mode_validation_context;\n   178→    }\n   179→\n   180→    if (!cert_validation_config->verifyCertificateSpkiList().empty()) {\n   181→      for (const auto& hash : 187→      }\n   188→      verify_mode = verify_mode_validation_context;\n   189→    }\n   190→  }\n   191→\n   192→  return verify_mode;\n   193→}\n   194→\n   195→bool DefaultCertValidator::verifyCertAndUpdateStatus(\n   196→    X509* leaf_cert, const Network::TransportSocketOptions* transport_socket_options,\n   197→    Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus& detailed_status, std::string* error_details,\n   198→    uint8_t* out_alert) {\n   199→  Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus validated =\n   200→      verifyCertificate(leaf_cert,\n   201→                        transport_socket_options != nullptr\n   202→                            ? transport_socket_options->verifySubjectAltNameListOverride()\n   203→                            : 211→  // If `trusted_ca` exists, it is already verified in the code above.                   ? validated != Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus::Failed\n   217→                           : validated == Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus::Validated;\n   218→\n   219→  return (allow_untrusted_certificate_ || success);\n   220→}\n   221→\n   222→Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus\n   223→DefaultCertValidator::verifyCertificate(X509* cert, const std::vector<std::string>& verify_san_list,\n   224→                                        const std::vector<SanMatcherPtr>& subject_alt_name_matchers,\n   225→                                        std::string* error_details, uint8_t* out_alert) {\n   226→  Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus validated = Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus::NotValidated;\n   227→  if (!verify_san_list.empty()) {\n   228→    if Envoy::Ssl::ClientValidationStatus::Validated;\n   275→  }\n   276→\n   277→  return validated;\n   278→}\n   279→\n   280→ValidationResults DefaultCertValidator::doVerifyCertChain(\n   281→ DefaultCertValidator::verifyCertificateSpkiList(\n   380→    X509* cert, const std::vector<std::vector<uint8_t>>& expected_hashes) {\n   381→  X509_PUBKEY* pubkey = X509_get_X509_PUBKEY(cert);\n 400→  return false;\n   401→}\n   402→\n   403→bool DefaultCertValidator::verifyCertificateHashList(\n   404→    X509* cert, const std::vector<std::vector<uint8_t>>& expected_hashes) {\n   405→ }\n   415→  return false;\n   416→}\n   417→\n   418→void DefaultCertValidator::updateDigestForSessionId(bssl::ScopedEVP_MD_CTX& md,\n   419→                                                    uint8_t hash_buffer[EVP_MAX_MD_SIZE],\n   420→                                                    unsigned hash_length) {\n   421→  int rc;\n   422→\n   423→  // Hash all the settings that affect whether the server will allow/accept\n   424→  // the client connection. This ensures that the client is always validated against\n   425→  // the correct settings, even if session resumption across different listeners\n   426→  // is enabled.\n   427→  if (ca_cert_ != nullptr) {\n   428→    rc = X509_digest(ca_cert_.get(), EVP_sha256(), hash_buffer, &hash_length);\n   429→    RELEASE_ASSERT(rc == 1, Utility::getLastCryptoError().value_or(\"\"));\n   430→    RELEASE_ASSERT(hash_length == SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH,\n   431→                   fmt::format(\"invalid SHA256 hash length {}\", hash_length));\n   432→\n   433→    rc = EVP_DigestUpdate(md.get(), hash_buffer, hash_length);\n   434→    RELEASE_ASSERT(rc == 1, Utility::getLastCryptoError().value_or(\"\"));\n   435→  }\n   436→\n   437→  for (const auto& hash : verify_certificate_hash_list_) {\n sizeof(std::remove_reference<decltype(hash)>::type::value_type));\n   441→    RELEASE_ASSERT(rc == 1, Utility::getLastCryptoError().value_or(\"\"));\n   442→  }\n   443→\n   444→  for (const auto& sizeof(std::remove_reference<decltype(hash)>::type::value_type));\n   448→    RELEASE_ASSERT(rc == 1, Utility::getLastCryptoError().value_or(\"\"));\n   449→  }\n   450→\n   451→  rc = config_->onlyVerifyLeafCertificateCrl();\n   476→    rc = EVP_DigestUpdate(md.get(), &only_leaf_crl, sizeof(only_leaf_crl));\n   477→    RELEASE_ASSERT(rc == 1, Utility::getLastCryptoError().value_or(\"\"));\n   478→  }\n   479→}\n   480→\n   481→absl::Status DefaultCertValidator::addClientValidationContext(SSL_CTX* ctx,\n   482→                                                              bool require_client_cert) {\n   483→  if (config_ == nullptr || config_->caCert().empty()) {\n   484→    return absl::OkStatus();\n   485→  }\n   486→\n   487→  bssl::UniquePtr<BIO> bio(\n   488→      BIO_new_mem_buf(const_cast<char*>(config_->caCert().data()), config_->caCert().size()));\n   489→  RELEASE_ASSERT(bio != nullptr, \"\");\n   490→  // Based on BoringSSL's SSL_add_file_cert_subjects_to_stack().\n   491→  // Use a generic lambda to be compatible with BoringSSL before and after\n   492→  // https://boringssl-review.googlesource.com/c/boringssl/+/56190\n   493→  bssl::UniquePtr<STACK_OF(X509_NAME)> list(\n   494→      sk_X509_NAME_new([](auto* a, auto* b) -> int { return X509_NAME_cmp(*a, *b); }));\n   495→  RELEASE_ASSERT(list != nullptr, \"\");\n   496→  for (;;) {\n   497→    bssl::UniquePtr<X509> cert(PEM_read_bio_X509(bio.get(), nullptr, nullptr, nullptr));\n   498→    if (cert == nullptr) {\n   499→      break;\n   500→    }\n   501→    X509_NAME* name = X509_get_subject_name(cert.get());\n   502→    if (name == nullptr) {\n   503→      return absl::InvalidArgumentError(absl::StrCat(\n   504→          \"Failed to load trusted client CA certificates from \", config_->caCertPath()));\n   505→    }\n   506→    // Check for duplicates.\n   507→    if (sk_X509_NAME_find(list.get(), nullptr, name)) {\n   508→      continue;\n   509→    }\n   510→    bssl::UniquePtr<X509_NAME> name_dup(X509_NAME_dup(name));\n   511→    if (name_dup == nullptr || !sk_X509_NAME_push(list.get(), name_dup.release())) {\n   512→      return absl::InvalidArgumentError(absl::StrCat(\n   513→          \"Failed to load trusted client CA certificates from \", config_->caCertPath()));\n   514→    }\n   515→  }\n   516→\n   517→  // Check for EOF.\n   518→  const uint32_t err = ERR_peek_last_error();\n   519→  if (ERR_GET_LIB(err) == ERR_LIB_PEM && ERR_GET_REASON(err) == PEM_R_NO_START_LINE) {\n   520→    ERR_clear_error();\n   521→  } else {\n   522→    return absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   523→        absl::StrCat(\"Failed to load trusted client CA certificates from \", config_->caCertPath()));\n   524→  }\n   525→  SSL_CTX_set_client_CA_list(ctx, list.release());\n   526→\n   527→  if (require_client_cert) {\n   528→    SSL_CTX_set_verify(ctx, SSL_VERIFY_PEER | SSL_VERIFY_FAIL_IF_NO_PEER_CERT, nullptr);\n   529→  }\n   530→  // Set the verify_depth\n   531→  if (config_->maxVerifyDepth().has_value()) {\n   532→ SSL_CTX_set_max_proto_version(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), config.maxProtocolVersion());\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(rc == 1, Utility::getLastCryptoError().value_or(\"\"));\n\n    if cipher and try them each individually in\n      // order to attempt to log which specific one failed. Example of config.cipherSuites():\n      // \"-ALL:[ECDHE-ECDSA-AES128-GCM-SHA256|ECDHE-ECDSA-CHACHA20-POLY1305]:ECDHE-ECDSA-AES128-SHA\".\n      //\n      // \"-\" is both an operator when in the leading position of a token (-ALL: don't allow this\n      // cipher), and the common separator in names (ECDHE-ECDSA-AES128-GCM-SHA256). Don't split on\n      // it because it will separate pieces of the same cipher. When it is a leading character, it\n      // is removed below.\n      std::vector<absl::string_view> ciphers =\n          StringUtil::splitToken(config.cipherSuites(), \":+![|]\", false);\n      std::vector<std::string> bad_ciphers;\n      for (const auto& cipher : ciphers) {\n        std::string cipher_str(cipher);\n\n        if (absl::StartsWith(cipher_str, \"-\")) {\n          cipher_str.erase(cipher_str.begin());\n        }\n\n        if (!SSL_CTX_set_strict_cipher_list(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), cipher_str.c_str())) {\n          bad_ciphers.push_back(cipher_str);\n        }\n      }\n      creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n          fmt::format(\"Failed to initialize cipher suites {}. As a client, SSL_VERIFY_NONE means to verify the certificate (which will fail\n        // without trust anchors), save the result in the session ticket, but otherwise continue\n        // with the handshake. But Envoy actually wants it to accept all certificates. The\n        // disadvantage of using SSL_VERIFY_NONE is that it records the verify_result, which Envoy\n        // never queries but gets saved in session tickets, and tries to find an anchor that isn't\n        // there. And also it differs from server side behavior of SSL_VERIFY_NONE which won't\n        // even request client certs. So, instead, we should configure a callback to skip\n        // validation and always supply the callback to boring SSL.\n        SSL_CTX_set_custom_verify(ctx, verify_mode, customVerifyCallback);\n must_staple_ext_value = \"\\x30\\x3\\x02\\x01\\x05\";\n      auto must_staple = Utility::getCertificateExtensionValue(*ctx.cert_chain_, tls_feature_ext);\n      if (must_staple == must_staple_ext_value) {\n        ctx.is_must_staple_ = true;\n      }\n\n      bssl::UniquePtr<EVP_PKEY> public_key(X509_get_pubkey(ctx.cert_chain_.get()));\n      const int pkey_id = larger keys.\n        const RSA* rsa_public_key = EVP_PKEY_get0_RSA(public_key.get());\n        // Since we checked the key type above, this should be valid.\n        ASSERT(rsa_public_key != nullptr);\n        const unsigned rsa_key_length = RSA_bits(rsa_public_key);\n#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n        if (rsa_key_length != 2048 && rsa_key_length != 3072 && rsa_key_length != 4096) {\n
